Commemoration Week of the Central Government and National Government 63

Central Party Headquarters: The Central Party Headquarters held Premier's Commemoration Week at 9:00 AM on the 30th. Central Committee members Chiang Kai-shek, Shao Yuanchong, Ma Chaojun, Yu Jingtang, Chen Lifu, and others, as well as party officials and guests, totaling over 800 people, attended. After Chiang Kai-shek, the chairman, led the ceremony, he made the following report: "Yesterday, I attended the memorial ceremony for the revolutionary martyrs and felt a myriad of emotions. The March 29th Uprising can be said to be a great memorial for the promotion of revolutionary integrity. This revolutionary spirit demonstrates a complete dedication to the principles and the nation, without absolutely mixing in a trace of personal selfishness or prejudice. Therefore, it was able to sow the foundation for later success and leave behind a great influence. We, the survivors, should not only continue their legacy but also promote and develop their cause to fully realize the goals of the revolution. The entire history of the Party is created by the sacrifice and struggle of each party member, and the revolutionary history of each comrade must also be supported by the entire body. For example, Chen Jiongming, he participated in the March 29th Uprising. At that time, the general comrades were extremely hopeful of him, and even Premier gave him much leniency. Unexpectedly, since the seventh year of the Republic, Chen Jiongming's actions often contradicted the Premier's, clearly aiming to achieve his selfish and self-interested goals. Not only did he not work hard for the revolution, but he also wanted to obstruct it. The Premier, in order to safeguard the overall revolutionary situation, wanted to restrain him and remove him from office several times, but the general comrades within the Party expressed opposition. Later, Chen Jiongming's rebellious actions became evident, openly commanding rebel soldiers to attack the Guanyinshan Presidential Palace, and the Premier narrowly escaped disaster. This clear rebellion is something that any person with blood would find infuriating, but there were still comrades who secretly discussed that the Premier should not have pushed Chen Jiongming too hard. This completely proves that the revolutionary comrades at that time did not clearly distinguish between public and private matters, only knowing personal feelings and disregarding the principles and the Party and the nation. If everyone could have clearly distinguished between public and private matters at that time and followed Comrade Zhu Zhixin's proposal early on, then the overall revolutionary situation would not have suffered a serious setback, preventing the Premier from witnessing the success of the revolution in his own lifetime. Moreover, Chen Jiongming had participated in the glorious March 29th Uprising. If the comrades had known earlier to love people with virtue and not to act with personal feelings and friendships, then Chen Jiongming would not have cut himself off from the Party. Chen Jiongming's later failure and disgrace were not necessarily due to the general comrades failing to preserve his past history for him. Revolution is a difficult and serious undertaking that cannot tolerate any setbacks. Therefore, we should completely emulate the spirit of the martyrs of Huanghuagang, being public-minded and forgetting private concerns, thinking about the interests of the overall situation and the seriousness of right and wrong. Otherwise, even with a very great leader like our Premier, the revolution will still inevitably suffer setbacks. A revolutionary party is not without emotions. The unity of our Party is especially based on the affectionate and sincere solidarity between comrades. However, the emotions that our Party speaks of should be completely based on the great cause of the revolution. We should first ask about the public interest and then about personal friendships. In short, revolution is an eternal struggle. The first is to recognize where the great cause lies, and the second is to constantly strive. We, in commemorating the martyrs of Huanghuagang, feel that the preservation of revolutionary history is not an easy task. We must strive diligently and relentlessly, not caring for our own safety, and comrades must especially be public-minded and selfless, completely责勉 each other with righteousness. Then, the revolutionary history of our Party will be promoted and developed day by day, and the goals of the revolution will be achieved. Also, our most important recent task is the National Assembly on May 5th. The Premier's dying testament was to hold a National Assembly and abolish the unequal treaties, two major events. The only important cases in the National Assembly are the abolition of unequal treaties and the provisional constitution for the period of political tutelage. These two matters are at the critical juncture of life and death for our Chinese nation. Our party members and the people of the whole country should pay close attention to these two points and quickly express their own opinions to contribute to the Party and the nation to determine the Party and the nation's long-term plan. Especially regarding the abolition of unequal treaties, we can recognize the true attitudes of various countries in this movement to abolish unequal treaties in the thirty-five days before the National Assembly. Which is our friend? Which country is our enemy? Which country is oppressing us? Which country is helping us? And we can determine this. We hope that the people of the whole country and all party comrades will pay extra attention to this point." The ceremony then concluded and the attendees dispersed.

National Government: The National Government held Premier's Commemoration Week in the Great Hall at 10:00 AM on the same morning. Chiang Kai-shek, Yu Youren, Shao Yuanchong, Li Yuying, Zhang Renjie, Wang Zhengting, Liu Shangqing, Ru Yuli, He Yaozu, Xu Tingyao, Ge Kengen, Chen Shaokuan, Chen Yi, Zhou Yawei, and other officials and staff of the National Government, totaling over 300 people, attended. After Chairman Chiang Kai-shek led the ceremony, Shao Yuanchong gave a speech, stating that in the Premier's teachings, he saw that political reform had an important principle, namely, "everyone should be given their due talent." The Premier also had a detailed explanation of this. Even if everyone is educated and encouraged properly, using their talent appropriately, then politics can be managed and social undertakings can be developed. Regarding educating people properly, except for the disabled, if they can be cultivated properly, whether they are intelligent or foolish, they can all be used to serve the world. Under the current Party rule, all politics are based on the Three Principles of the People and the Premier's teachings, formulated into policies and guidelines, and handed over by the Party to the government to implement. The government implements the policies and guidelines set by the Party step by step, which can show the spirit of the Party. However, political reform must also be done in order of priority and urgency, completed in sequence according to human and financial resources. Therefore, in education, talents must also be cultivated according to needs. In the past, many students who returned from studying abroad could not express their talents due to various reasons, which was not economical. Now, the urgency of various undertakings in the country should be considered, and then various practical talents should be cultivated according to this principle. In the recent years, the following matters should be actively worked on: (1) Completing local autonomy as the basis for political tutelage. (2) Popularizing education and then cultivating various specialized talents. (3) Developing and improving agriculture to enrich the people's food supply. We must gather the human and financial resources of the whole country in the recent years to make significant achievements in the above three undertakings, and then carry out other undertakings as appropriate. The government uses extremely economical methods to use human and financial resources, and education also follows this guideline for cultivation. In this way, people can make full use of their talents, making the political foundation more stable, and cultural and construction undertakings will gradually develop. Then, by dividing labor and cooperating, everything can be completed. The full text of the speech is being organized.

Inauguration of Party Committees in Northeast Provinces and Regions 64

Shenyang Correspondence: The Party Affairs Steering Committee and Party Affairs Special Commissioners of the Northeast provinces and regions held an oath-taking ceremony at the Liaoning Provincial Party Headquarters on the 26th. From around 9:00 AM that morning, guests from all walks of life arrived in succession, totaling over a thousand people. However, there were only six hundred seats inside the venue, so many who arrived later stood outside the venue. At 10:20 AM, Zhang Xueliang arrived, and after getting out of the car, he went to the reception room for a brief rest before ringing the bell to start the meeting. Zhang, along with oath supervisor Wu Tiecheng, Central Committee member Zhang Ji, and special commissioners from the five provinces and regions, entered the auditorium in single file. The master of ceremonies announced the following rituals: (1) Stand at attention (play music), (2) Sing the Party Song, (3) Bow three times to the national flag, Party flag, and Sun Yat-sen's portrait, (4) The oath supervisor respectfully reads Sun Yat-sen's will, (5) Silent meditation for three minutes, (6) Those taking the oath raise their right hands and read the oath (divided into groups by province: 1. Liaoning, 2. Jilin, 3. Heilongjiang, 4. Rehe, 5. Harbin. Except for Xi Qia and Gu Gengye from the Jilin Committee, and Tang Yulin from the Rehe Committee, all others were present), (7) The oath supervisor (Wu Tiecheng) delivers a speech, (8) The person taking the oath (represented by Zhang Xueliang) gives a reply, (9) Ceremony concludes (play music), (10) Take a photo. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 noon.

In the afternoon, at 2:00 PM, a joint meeting of the Party Committees of the five provinces and regions was held to discuss future work policies. At 4:00 PM, the Liaoning Provincial Party Committee held its first meeting to discuss internal organization and implementation plans, which lasted until 6:00 PM in the evening before adjourning. The appended speeches are as follows:

Wu Tiecheng's Speech: Respected comrades and guests, today

is the inauguration ceremony for the Party Affairs Steering Committee and

Special Commissioners of the four Northeast provinces and the Harbin Special Region. It is also the establishment of the Liaoning Provincial Party Headquarters. This ceremony is very grand, a bright and splendid page in the history of national salvation and nation-building. Although the Northeast Party Headquarters was established late today, the Northeast comrades and the Northeast people have participated in revolutionary practical work for twenty years and contributed a great deal to the revolutionary movement, promoting the current unified and peaceful situation. As for why the Northeast Party Headquarters was established only today, it was because of the Sino-Russian War the year before last and the Feng-Yan Rebellion last year. For three or four years, Northeast comrades defended the country against foreign aggression and promoted national unity and peace. It was purely a matter of timing that it was established today.

Tiecheng is very honored to represent the Central Committee and participate in this grand event. I would also like to take this opportunity to say a few words on behalf of the comrades of the Central Committee. The comrades of the Central Committee know that the Northeast comrades have a great force in the history and spirit of the revolution. The Northeast comrades and the Northeast people continue to work hard and sacrifice for the revolution. It is very important to review the past facts. Although there have been several gaps in the middle, efforts have always been consistent. After the establishment of the Northeast Party Headquarters, it is hoped that all comrades will embrace two directions: (1) Spirit, (2) Material. The most important thing is that because it was in the military period before, of course, in the destructive period, since the military period has reached the tutelage period, we should all go on the road to construction. When President Sun Yat-sen was dying, he repeatedly told us to "peacefully struggle to save China." Now that the obstacles have been removed, we must use peace to save China, use the spirit of peace to do construction work, and use the Three Principles of the People to promote China. Since 400 million Chinese compatriots know that the Three Principles of the People is the doctrine of national salvation, we should think of ways to make our compatriots thoroughly understand the greatness of the Three Principles of the People. The national character of the people of Northeast China is simple and honest. Northeast comrades work hard in propaganda, and we believe that the Three Principles of the People is the doctrine of saving China and building China. I believe that Northeast Party affairs will inevitably be more successful than other provinces. President Sun Yat-sen's Three Principles of the People is the culmination of ancient and modern China and foreign countries. President Sun Yat-sen also said that the Chinese people are the way of the king. What is called the way of the king is to convince people with virtue, which is different from the way of hegemony, which is to convince people with force. President Sun Yat-sen's Three Principles of the People relies purely on benevolence and righteousness. For example, Yao and Shun ruled the country and the world was public. In other words, they served the public. The Three Principles of the People is to call on the people to serve the society. Revolutionary comrades take serving the society as their duty. Our comrades have firmly believed in the Three Principles of the People. From then on, our actions should take the country as the premise, not the purpose of seizing. This is the starting point of the Three Principles of the People. We should work hard to promote it to the people of Northeast China. As for the seven basic movements of party members, they are afforestation, literacy, baojia, sanitation, national goods, roads, cooperation, etc. These seven tasks are to express the Three Principles of the People in both propaganda and political aspects. In other words, it is to be consistent in words and deeds. Furthermore, when it comes to the relationship between the Party Headquarters and the government, Tiecheng represents the Central Committee's comrades and says a few more words. In the past, many personnel of the Party Headquarters in various provinces, counties, and cities were found to be acting immaturely, causing the general public to lose their sympathy for the Party. However, the comrades who run the Party cannot be trained well in a short period of time. After the Kuomintang unified China, it did not prepare many talents for running the Party and distributed them to various places, because those who believe in the Party's doctrine and the talents for running the Party are absolutely two different things. In the past, many disputes occurred between the Party and the local government and the people because of this reason. It is hoped that the Northeast comrades should thoroughly realize and recognize the reasons for this kind of mistake. Speaking of the Party and the government are two systems, the Central Party Headquarters is supervising the National Government. Under the National Government is the provincial government, and the provincial government controls the county and municipal governments. The Party Headquarters in the provinces, cities, and counties can only supervise the local government's implementation of the central government's laws and regulations and report to the Central Committee whether they have violated any acts. The Central Committee notifies the National Government to correct the errors and cannot exercise supervisory tasks. On the one hand, it is only responsible for propaganda to the people, so that the people can understand the central government's policies. In the past, such unfortunate disputes as those that occurred in the Party Headquarters in various counties of Hebei Province should not be seen in the future. At the same time, the Party and the government should be united as one, so that the construction cause can be free from obstacles. I talked to Deputy Commander Zhang about running the Party two years ago. At that time, Deputy Commander Zhang had an ambition and said to me that if the Northeast runs the Party, it must be better than all other provinces and counties, so that the Party affairs in the Northeast can catch up later. At that time, I greatly admired Comrade Zhang Hanqing's understanding of the Party was very profound and persevering, and I believed that although the Northeast Party Headquarters was established later, it would inevitably catch up later after it was completed. The comrades of the Central Committee also made comments and all twelve points believed that the future achievements of the Northeast Party affairs would be able to catch up later. Today, Tiecheng participated in the inauguration ceremony of the Party Affairs Steering Committee of the four Northeast provinces and the Party Affairs Special Commissioner of Harbin, and I am very honored, and I wish the Party Affairs workers and the people of Northeast China to work together.

Zhang Ji's Speech: After Wu Tiecheng's speech, Zhang Ji gave a speech, saying briefly that today is the inauguration of the Party Steering Committee of the Northeast provinces and regions and the establishment ceremony of the Liaoning Provincial Party Headquarters. I am very honored to participate in this grand and solemn event. My ancestral home is Hebei. I have been to Liaoning six times. I have always paid close attention to the Northeast because You, Yan, Liao, and Jin are dependent on each other. Looking at the glorious history of the people of Northeast China in the past, they are now deeply insulted and oppressed by imperialists and are struggling and fighting every day. The reason why the imperialists are carrying out aggression is purely a national problem. It must be known that our nation is a mixture of Han, Manchu, Mongol, Hui, and Tibetan, and they are not separated from each other. Moreover, the national spirit of our country is strong, persevering, and hardworking, and it is crowned by all countries in the world with such an excellent and great nation. No matter what imperialists carry out oppression, the result will eventually be failure. To seek national rejuvenation, we must have self-confidence. Today, the Liaoning Provincial Party Headquarters is established, I hope you will lead the people to take on the glorious history of our motherland and work together to strive to promote the great spirit of our nation.

Northeast Reclamation Superintendent Goes Abroad to Inspect Land Reclamation Policies of Various Countries 65

Publishes Account of Reclamation Efforts and Inspection Opinions Before Departure

Shenyang Correspondence: Zou Zuohua, the Superintendent of Land Reclamation in the Xing'an Region of Northeast China, has spared no effort in handling land reclamation affairs in recent years and has now achieved excellent results. Recently, in view of the need to learn from Europe and the United States in land reclamation, he requested and was approved by Zhang Xueliang, Commander of the Northeast Border Defense, to travel to European and American countries to inspect land reclamation policies. The planned trip is for one year, with monthly travel expenses of 10,000 yuan. Only Secretary Xu Kechang and Liu Mingjiu will accompany him. All matters related to the Land Reclamation Superintendent will be the responsibility of Chief Executive Gao Renfu. The following is a record of Mr. Zou's conversation at the time of his departure: "Since the Northeast Army entered the customs in the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, at that time, the reorganization was implemented. I was the Artillery Commander and requested to bring a part of the army to the border to try out land reclamation, on the one hand, to develop national resources and enrich border defense and security, and on the other hand, to promote agricultural and industrial undertakings, adjust the domestic surplus population, and eliminate the unemployed demobilized army for productive undertakings. At the same time, I also want to help Mongolian compatriots develop their various undertakings. However, I was originally a soldier and have little knowledge of politics and scholarship. Moreover, there is no precedent for land reclamation in China, and even the current central government has no overall plan for land reclamation. Therefore, for the past two years, I have been constantly working hard on land reclamation, but I still feel that the strategies are insufficient. Therefore, I have long planned to have the opportunity to go abroad to inspect once as a reference for future land reclamation. Furthermore, the funding for land reclamation is now extremely difficult. Various large-scale constructions such as road construction and mining cannot be carried out according to plan. If this continues, the future of land reclamation will be in unimaginable danger. If it unfortunately fails, it will not be important to me personally, but I am afraid that it will affect the future of land reclamation in China. At the same time, the Chinese people will also regard land reclamation as a daunting task. As a result, all national resources, border defense security, and a number of unemployed people in the country will be in a dangerous situation. Therefore, the relationship is really great, so today is a time of great urgency. We must strive to find a way out. This time, I went abroad to persuade overseas Chinese capitalists to invest in the Xing'an area to help the development of land reclamation. I have had this idea for a long time. In the past, because land reclamation was in its initial stage, everything was not yet in place, so I did not dare to let go and go abroad immediately. Now, various land reclamation facilities have taken shape. There should be no delay during the short period of time I am away. I began to ask Commander Zhang to fulfill my long-cherished wish for foreign inspection. After going abroad, all the affairs of the Land Reclamation Office have been entrusted to a competent person to act as an agent, and it can be carried out according to the fixed plan. All my itinerary dates and inspection steps have not yet been determined, so I cannot publish them for the time being. I will wait until I return to the country to make all the process and gains public to the whole country as a reference for my land reclamation and as a blueprint for all future land reclamation undertakings in China. Finally, the conclusion is that this time I went abroad for land reclamation and did not stop land reclamation because of going abroad." (26th)

Sichuan Becomes Southwest Opium Center 67

Yunnan, Guizhou, and Gansu Opium Are All Shipped Out from Here

Yichang Is the Number One Export Market

Chongqing Correspondence: The length of time opium has been planted in Sichuan is well-known both at home and abroad. The name of Sichuan opium has spread far and wide. Farmers rely on it for their livelihoods and to cope with high taxes and levies. Armies rely on it for their maintenance and expansion. According to a recent survey, the counties with the most opium cultivation are Fengdu, Fuling, Liangshan, Dianjiang, Kaixian, Suiding, Youyang, and Xiushan in eastern Sichuan; Pingshan, Leibo, Mabian, Xichang, and Yazhou in southern Sichuan; Songpan, Lifan, Maoxian, Guanxian, and Qionglai in western Sichuan; and Tongjiang, Nanjiang, Bazhong, Nanbu, and Xichong in northern Sichuan. These are all well-known special product areas. The provinces that import into Sichuan are Yunnan and Guizhou. Yunnan opium is imported through Xufu, Guizhou opium is imported through Qijiang and Fuling, and Gansu opium is imported through Bikou. Chengdu and Xikang opium are imported into Chengdu through Yazhou. A small portion of the opium produced locally in Sichuan and imported from other provinces is consumed in Sichuan, and the majority is still transshipped and exported to other provinces. Yichang is the number one export market for Sichuan opium. A relatively small number of opium is exported from Suiding and Chengkou to Xiangyang, Fancheng, and Laokou in Hubei. The Yangtze River coast and Henan, Hebei, Shandong and other provinces are all sales markets for Sichuan opium. Therefore, the number of people engaged in investing in the opium trade is increasing day by day, and it occupies a strong position in the entire Sichuan business community. The special industry chambers of commerce in Yichang, Chongqing, Wanxian and other places can be used to

see the integrity of its organization. Recently, even brokers have organized a special industry neutral merchants' association, which is enough to prove the general situation of opium production and sales in Sichuan.

Soviet Russia Traffics Grain from Northern Manchuria 68

Direct Loading and Export from Fujin

The Conspiracy of the Soviet-Russian Grain and Stone Company

Undermining the Economy and Commerce of Northern Manchuria

Harbin Correspondence: The Binjiang Chamber of Commerce heard on the 23rd that Soviet Russia was buying miscellaneous grains and soybean oil in Fujin, downstream of the Songhua River, and shipping them out of the country, so it telegraphed the Fujin County Chamber of Commerce to inquire about the truth. That evening, it received a reply from Fujin stating that the Russian purchase of oil and grain was in accordance with the provincial order to levy a 5% duty on top of various taxes for export. The Binjiang Chamber of Commerce considered the telegram to be too brief, so it invited the Harbin Chamber of Commerce, oil mills, flour mills, grain merchants, grocery stores, and other groups to hold a joint meeting at the Binjiang City Chamber of Commerce to discuss the government's approach. As a result, it was decided to first telegraph the provincial government to inquire about the details of the matter and then deliberate after receiving a reply. In addition, the entire navigation industry also held a meeting at the Navigation Bureau to discuss the matter and decided to follow the attitude of each group. It is heard that the reason why the Russian purchase of oil and grain is directly exported is that the Russian government established a grain and stone purchasing company in Harbin in February this year with a capital of 2 million gold rubles to specialize in buying soybean and grain for sale to Europe and the United States to make profits. The reason why the special products of Northern Manchuria cannot be exported is not that the fundamental market price is higher than that of Europe and the United States, nor that the special product merchants of Europe and the United States are unwilling to buy them. The reason is that the freight of the East Railway is too high and the grain price plus the freight does not meet the market price of Europe and the United States. Russian merchants buy at low prices and ship directly from Fujin to Russia by ship or travel overland through the Ussuri Road to Siberia and enter Europe, or ship by sea from Vladivostok to the United States to earn multiple profits. Because of the purchase of grain, they can also take the opportunity to drive ships into our inland rivers to share the navigation rights of the Songhua River and import Russian goods through the river, which is a multiple benefit. This move was contacted by the Russian Consul stationed in Harbin with the Jilin Provincial Authorities. The Jilin Authorities did not carefully examine it and hastily allowed Fujin to be a rich area of special products in Northern Manchuria. The economy and commerce of grain and stone have always relied on Harbin for transshipment and export. Russia's interception and purchase there has cut off the source of goods and products from Harbin and Northern Manchuria.

It is quite destructive to the production and commercial system of Harbin, so it is extremely worthy of attention. (24th)

Gao Ying's Appeal Case Judgement 69

Original Judgment Revoked, Innocent of Opium Portion

Official Misconduct Portion Sentenced to One Year and Four Months

Sun Yuan Sentenced to Two Years for Opium Portion

After the Supreme Court sent Gao Ying's case of assisting in opium trafficking and official misconduct back for retrial, the Jiangsu Higher Court held a hearing on the 26th and announced the end of the debate. Today is the date of the verdict. At 2:15 PM, Chief Justice Lin Dawen of the Criminal Division One ascended the Fourth Tribunal (because the First Tribunal was holding an examination and watchman) and brought Gao Ying and Sun Yuan to the court to inquire about their age and place of origin, and then read the main text of the verdict as follows: "The original judgment on Gao Ying and Sun Yuan is revoked. Gao Ying is sentenced to one year and four months of imprisonment for soliciting bribes in the course of his duties, and fined 1,400 yuan. The number of days of custody before the determination of the judgment shall be converted into one day for every two days of imprisonment. If the fine is converted into imprisonment, it shall be calculated at three yuan per day, but the term of imprisonment shall not exceed one year. He is innocent of the opium portion. Sun Yuan is sentenced to two years of imprisonment for assisting in the sale of opium, and fined 2,000 yuan. The number of days of custody before the determination of the judgment shall be converted into one day for every two days of imprisonment. If the fine is converted into imprisonment, it shall be calculated at three yuan per day, but the term of imprisonment shall not exceed one year." After the judgment was pronounced, Sun Yuan declared an appeal. Gao Ying also expressed an appeal and said that the purpose of the appeal was not to fight for civil rights, but because he was not willing to submit to the facts. In addition, Gao's wife, Liao Suqiu, has been seriously ill recently, but it may not be easy to arrange for medical treatment outside of bail.

Arrest of Suspects in the Kaiyuan Township Robbery Case: It has been learned that the Su Shunji Trough Workshop in Heliekou, Kaiyuan Township, Fourth District, was robbed by more than ten bandits at midnight on the 20th of this month, resulting in a loss of 600 yuan. It is now known that Liu Chunlan, the chief of the Ninth Branch of the Public Security Bureau in charge of the area, led police officers on a patrol yesterday morning around 9:00 am. They saw a person looking flustered near the Mao toilet behind Su Shunji. The person hid in the toilet, pretending to relieve themselves. Director Liu of the branch suspected the person's behavior and immediately arrested him, bringing him back to the bureau for interrogation. I also cut the telephone lines to prevent reporting." After receiving the confession, Director Liu immediately prepared a document and submitted it to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Rampant Meningitis in the Urban Area: Since the beginning of spring in this area, the weather has been erratic, with sudden cold and hot spells. As a result, infectious diseases are rampant in the city, such as diphtheria and colds, with many sufferers. Meningitis is especially rampant, and its onset is extremely rapid, with little chance of recovery if treatment is delayed. For example, a Zhang woman, aged 17, residing in the workers' quarters of the Jiatai Silk Factory outside the East Gate, suddenly contracted the disease and died at 2:00 pm yesterday. At the same time, a Cai boy named Meigen, aged 9, residing in Wang Daoren Lane, also contracted the disease, and his condition is quite dangerous. His mother, Cai, was also infected and sought treatment at Tongren Hospital yesterday. In addition, Zhang, a child residing in Shuyuan Lane, Li Genbao (age 22) from Xicheng Foot, and Ms. Chen Huiying (age 18) from Dongting Town, and a Yang child named Kun Sheng (age 10) in Baer Lane in the city, also contracted meningitis. Except for Sun Kun Sheng, who has already died, the others are in critical condition and are currently receiving treatment at Tongren Hospital.

The Truth About the Case of the Wife Killed with a Pitchfork: Huang Rongchu, a villager from Cheng Tang near Yanqiao Town, Tianshang City, Fifth District, killed his wife, Shen Qinxian, with a pitchfork a few days ago. The murderer was caught on the spot and sent to the Public Security Branch for transfer to the County Court for interrogation and detention. It is now known that the reason for Huang Rongchu's murder of his wife was jealousy. The deceased, Shen Qinxian, had an affair with Gao Ziqing, who used to be a car manager at the Taichang Silk Factory outside the South Gate. Gao's wife, Shen, learned about this and informed Huang Rongchu, Qinxian's husband. Huang was furious upon hearing this, leading to the tragic event of killing his wife with a pitchfork. After learning about this, Gao Ziqing was also furious because his wife's jealousy had caused this great disaster. He took a kitchen knife the morning before yesterday and slashed at his wife, Shen, twice, but both missed. Neighbors snatched the kitchen knife away. However, Gao was still not satisfied and took a ladle, hitting Shen on the back of the head, causing blood to flow and Shen to collapse unconscious on the ground. Neighbors sent Shen to the hospital in the city for treatment and notified Shen's family to come and arrest Gao, sending him to the Eighth Branch of the Public Security Bureau. Director Zhou opened the court for preliminary interrogation and sent the case to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation yesterday.

Careless Electrical Fault at Yu Lun Silk Factory: The Yu Lun Silk Factory outside the South Gate of this area, north of Tieshu Bridge, was originally scheduled to start production on April 2nd. Therefore, raw materials (i.e., dried cocoons) have been transported back to the factory in recent days to meet the demand. As a result, there were many dried cocoons piled up in the warehouse. Unexpectedly, at around 1:00 am yesterday, an electrical fault occurred in the warehouse, and flames soared, making it impossible to approach. The fire brigades from various sections rushed to the scene and worked hard to put out the fire, but the goods stored in the warehouse were completely burned to ashes. Fortunately, the factory had fire insurance and has already telegraphed the Shanghai Insurance Company yesterday, requesting them to send personnel to Wuxi for inspection in order to receive compensation.

Education News

Important News 79

Fujian Salt

Monthly Allocation of 120,000 for Education Expenses

The Ministry of Finance previously approved the Fujian Provincial Government's request to allocate 140,000 yuan per month for education expenses after the salt surtax revenue was centralized. However, the current tax rate for Fujian salt is only 2 yuan per dan for the regular tax and 3 yuan for the surtax, which is disproportionate compared to other salt-producing areas. Furthermore, the expenses of 106,000 yuan per month for the administrative, inspection, and anti-smuggling agencies of the salt industry, as well as other temporary expenses, are all paid from the regular tax and are not the responsibility of the local government. Therefore, in June of the 17th year, the Fujian Finance Reorganization Committee decided that the salt affairs expenses were insufficient. The regulation attached to the outlines and measures for the distribution of the military quota, military expenses quota, and military-political expenses of Fujian included a provision to allocate 30,000 yuan per month from the salt surtax to supplement the salt affairs expenses. In October of last year, the ministry submitted a proposal to the Executive Yuan, which was decided at the 89th meeting. When the monthly revenue from the Fujian salt surtax is within 120,000 yuan, it should be fully allocated to education expenses. If it exceeds 120,000 yuan, subsidies may be provided according to the proposal. The provincial government of Fujian and the Ministry of Education have been notified accordingly. As for the seasonal fluctuations in salt tax revenue, it is inherently uncertain. After the centralization of salt surtax from various provinces, it is necessary to reorganize and reduce or exempt taxes. In the future, there will inevitably be changes, so it is impossible to use the current peak revenue as a standard. All education expenses to be allocated under the Fujian salt surtax should be based on the original proposal of the Executive Yuan's 89th resolution, with a fixed amount of 120,000 yuan per month, which is the fairest. The national treasury should allocate and issue 120,000 yuan per month after the revenue is recovered. The Ministry of Education has instructed the Fujian Department to inform them of this situation.

Ministry of Education's Instructions on Interpretation of Civil Servants 80

The Ministry of Education received a report from the Shaanxi Education Department stating that Zhang Buying, the magistrate of Zhongbu County, requested an interpretation of whether principals, teachers, and staff of primary and secondary schools below the senior primary level, as well as staff of educational institutions, are civil servants. The Ministry of Education instructed: It is understood that the term "civil servants" in the current Regulations for the Screening and Examination of Incumbent Civil Servants does not include principals and teachers of all levels of schools. However, the director of the county education bureau is an appointed official according to Article 17 of the County Organization Law and should be subject to screening and examination. The grade is determined by the education department of each province. If the actual salary of the director of the county education bureau is lower than the salary payable for the original grade, an explanation may be added when filling out the screening and examination form, and the grade in the official system does not need to be changed based on the actual salary. Other positions such as supervisors, clerks, and general affairs personnel who are clearly defined as appointed officials in the organizational regulations of the county education bureau should also be subject to screening and examination in accordance with the regulations. However, these organizational regulations are limited to those approved by the provincial government or the provincial education department. You should be informed and instructed accordingly.

A Glimpse of Tsinghua's New President, Wu Nanxuan (Ming) 81

Wu Nanxuan, the newly appointed president of National Tsinghua University, passed through Zhenjiang yesterday to visit relatives in Yangzhou. A reporter met him at the Zhenjiang Railway Station that evening and obtained the following glimpse:

(Question) Could you tell us about your appointment as the president of Tsinghua? (Answer) After returning to China, I was teaching at the Central Political School, and the responsibility was heavy. I wanted to give up my duties and voluntarily return to my alma mater, Fudan (graduated from Fudan and studied abroad), or other schools, just to teach from books and avoid a lot of trouble. Unexpectedly, a month ago, there was a proposal to appoint me as the president of Henan University. Before I could decline, I received the order to go to Tsinghua. I usually have no thoughts about Tsinghua in my mind, and Beijing was not the place where I wanted to teach. I insisted on declining, but I had to take on the responsibility temporarily. It was truly beyond my expectations. (Question) What do you think of the achievements of the former president, Luo? (Answer) Mr. Luo is decisive, has魄力 (a blend of drive and ambition), has ideas, and has knowledge. In recent years, there has been a lot of new construction in the school. (Question) Is it true that student representatives of the school have had a conversation with you, as reported in the Beijing Daily? (Answer) Their intention was nothing more than to inquire about the future school administration. I am naturally clumsy and only show sincerity to anyone I talk to. The opinions I expressed to the student representatives are the same as those I want to express to the central government: (1) I cannot have concrete proposals before I arrive at the school. (2) The foreseeable goals are to proceed with the original plan approved by President Chiang to rectify the school spirit and develop Tsinghua. (3) I hope that the school will develop evenly in the future. (4) I hope that students will not only seek progress in the intellectual aspect but also strive for all-round development in the moral aspect. (5) This trip puts personal interests aside and is based on openness and sincerity. I am naturally不喜欢 (dislike) using智巧 (cleverness and strategy), and I will not use智巧.智巧 (cleverness and strategy) sometimes ends, but sincerity can gain people's understanding. If the students' opinions do not go beyond the scope of what the school should prosper and reform, they should be adopted automatically. As for how to implement them concretely, there must be a standard after arriving in Beijing. (Question) What is the school's financial situation? (Answer) The regular expenses are more than 1 million, and the temporary expenses are also close to 1 million, totaling about 3 million. The source is the American Boxer Indemnity. However, the Boxer Indemnity has a completion time, so a certain amount of millions is allocated from the regular expenses each year as a fund. The principal and interest cannot be used. Currently, there are more than 9 million, and this fund can be increased in the future. This fund was formerly managed jointly by the government's Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Americans, but it is now managed by the Cultural Fund Management Office. (Question) When will you go to Beijing? (Answer) It has not been decided yet. At this point, the car had entered the station, so we hurriedly said goodbye.

The Education Department Strictly Orders Investigation

Ministry of Education Revises Regulations for Vocational Schools 84

Chapter 3: Finances and Equipment (Continued)

Article 10: The minimum amount of start-up funds and annual operating expenses for various vocational schools (start-up funds include construction costs, equipment costs, etc.) are tentatively set as shown in the table below:

Category Start-up Funds Annual Operating Expenses

Category A, No. 1, 2, 3, 4 200,000 yuan 100,000 yuan

Vocational Schools

11, 15, 16, etc.

Vocational Schools

13, 14, etc.

Vocational Schools

Category B, No. 1, 2, 6, 7, 100,000 yuan 80,000 yuan

8, etc. Vocational Schools

Category B, No. 3, 4, 5, etc. 60,000 yuan 50,000 yuan

Vocational Schools

Category C, Vocational Schools of all kinds 60,000 yuan 50,000 yuan

Category D, Medical Vocational Schools 150,000 yuan 100,000 yuan

Category D, Pharmaceutical Vocational Schools 100,000 yuan 80,000 yuan

Category D, Merchant Marine Vocational Schools 100,000 yuan 60,000 yuan

Category D, No. 3, 4, 5, 6 60,000 yuan 50,000 yuan

7, 9, etc. Vocational Schools

The operating expenses for each vocational school in the first year must each have at least two-thirds of the amount specified in this table. For industrial, agricultural, and commercial vocational schools with two or more departments, the amount of start-up funds and annual operating expenses should be determined based on the number and type of departments. If the departments are of the same nature, the amount may be appropriately reduced according to the standard set in this table.

Article 11: The annual equipment expansion fee for vocational schools should account for at least 15% of the operating expenses.

Article 12: The equipment standards for vocational schools will be determined separately.

Chapter 4: Examinations and Grades

Article 13: Vocational school examinations are divided into the following four types: 1. Entrance Examination 2. Temporary Examination 3. Semester Examination 4. Graduation Examination

Article 14: The entrance examination is organized by the Admissions Committee of the School Affairs Meeting and held before the start of each academic year.

Article 15: Temporary examinations are conducted by the teachers of each department at any time. At least one temporary examination must be held in each semester. The results of the temporary examination must be combined with the grades of lectures, notes, reading notes, and practice experiments to be calculated as the usual grades.

Article 16: Semester examinations are held by the principal in conjunction with the teachers at the end of the semester. The results of the semester examination must be combined with the usual grades to be calculated as the semester grades.

Article 17: The graduation examination is the semester examination for the final semester, but the examination subjects must be more than five, and at least three must include the entire academic year's curriculum. The graduation examination is organized by a committee composed of teachers from within the school and external experts appointed by the Ministry of Education. The principal is the chairman of the committee. Each subject's examination must have an external member participate within the possible scope. When necessary, the Ministry of Education may send personnel to supervise the examination.

Article 18: Students of Category A, B, and C vocational schools must practice in a corresponding place for several weeks during the summer or winter vacation each year. Those without this practice certificate may not graduate. The practice procedure is determined by each school, but it must be submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval.

Chapter 5: Supplementary Provisions

Article 19: Private vocational schools must comply with the Regulations for Private Schools in addition to these regulations.

Article 20: These regulations are formulated and promulgated by the Ministry of Education in accordance with Article 12 of the Vocational School Organization Law (End)

Municipal Education Bureau Director Xu Peihuang on 87

The Draft of the Municipal Education Administration's General Outline of a Speech

Xu Peihuang, director of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, gave a speech at the Qingnianhui at the invitation of the Municipal Research Association, outlining the general situation of education in Shanghai. The general situation has been published in various newspapers, but there were slight errors in the transcript (editor's note: the transcript was issued by the Xinsheng Society), which did not correspond to the original meaning of the speech. Yesterday, Xu specially spoke to reporters to correct this, saying that the speech at the time actually stated that all countries in the world have a certain direction for education. This direction must not only be suitable for the shortcomings of the country's society but also adapt to the world's trends of thought. Otherwise, even if the material civilization of the world progresses, it will be of little benefit to mankind. The educational policy of our country is based on Dr. Sun Yat-Sen's legacy, which shows that after restoring all the inherent national essence of our country, we must learn from the strengths of Europe and the United States. The educational policy of the Three Principles of the People is the only way to build education that is shifted from material construction to psychological construction to achieve social construction. This certain and unchangeable educational purpose is enough to change the past state of randomness and build a consistent spirit for the future. The implementation of the Three Principles of the People is urgently needed by our country's environment as the only good medicine to save our country from poverty and weakness, and those who promote its power and promote its spirit must devote themselves to the construction of Three Principles of the People education. Therefore, the education of the Three Principles of the People is the center of our efforts, and there is no other way out. Furthermore, the greatness of the education of the Three Principles of the People, its ultimate goal is not only to save our country but also to save the world and achieve world harmony.

In addition, there were omissions and errors in the number of schools mentioned in the speech. For example, there are actually 597 unregistered primary schools in this city, but the draft was mistakenly published as 59. The full text of the speech will be published later after it is sorted out by the Municipal Research Association and myself.

Local News

Shanghai-Yichang Air Route 101

Officially Inaugurated Today

Departs at 7 AM, Arrives in Yichang at 5 PM

Beijing-Pingjin Line Being Actively Arranged

The Shanghai-Yichang air route of the China National Aviation Corporation is officially inaugurated today for transporting mail and passengers. Flights will operate every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday, flying directly from Shanghai to Yichang. Flights will operate every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday, flying directly from Yichang to Shanghai. Between Shanghai and Hankou, flights will operate daily except on Mondays. The details heard are recorded as follows:

Departure This Morning: The Shanghai-Yichang air route is officially inaugurated at 7:00 AM this morning at the Longhua seaplane airport. The aircraft will be either the No. 3 Hankou or the No. 4 Jiujiang; the decision has not yet been made. The pilot has been confirmed as German pilot Gesto. Departing at 7:00 AM, it is expected to arrive in Hankou at 2:10 PM. At 2:45 PM, it will depart Hankou, piloted by American pilot Anlisen, and the original aircraft will fly to Yichang, expected to arrive at 5:10 PM. In the future, Anlisen and an American pilot, Shatoli, will take turns flying the Hankou-Yichang section.

Passengers Flying to Yichang: Those taking the flight to Yichang this morning include Mr. McKinney, Mr. Weistof, and Mr. Fengte, representatives of an American air transport company, who are going directly to Yichang to proceed to Chongqing to investigate air transport conditions. As for mail, because the outside world is not yet fully aware, it is feared that there will not be much. The local Postal Administration has already issued a notice accepting airmail bound for Yichang.

Flight Times: The official flight times are as follows: A. Westbound Flight (1) Shanghai departs at 7:00 AM (2) Nanjing arrives at 9:15 AM, departs at 9:30 AM (3) Wuhu arrives at 10:05 AM, departs at 10:10 AM (4) Anqing arrives at 11:20 AM, departs at 11:25 AM (5) Jiujiang arrives at 12:25 PM, departs at 12:40 PM (6) Hankou arrives at 2:10 PM (The above is the Shanghai-Hankou line; flights operate daily except on Mondays.) (1) Hankou departs at 2:45 PM (2) Shashi arrives at 4:15 PM, departs at 4:25 PM (3) Yichang arrives at 5:10 PM (The above is the Hankou-Yichang line; flights operate every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday.) B. Eastbound Flight (1) Yichang departs at 6:00 AM (2) Shashi arrives at 6:45 AM, departs at 6:55 AM (3) Hankou arrives at 8:25 AM (The above is the Hankou-Yichang line; flights operate every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday.) (1) Hankou departs at 9:00 AM (2) Jiujiang arrives at 10:30 AM, departs at 10:45 AM (3) Anqing arrives at 11:45 AM, departs at 11:50 AM (4) Wuhu arrives at 1:00 PM, departs at 1:05 PM (5) Nanjing departs at 1:40 PM (6) departs at 1:55 PM Shanghai arrives at 4:10 PM (The above is the Shanghai-Hankou line.)

Passenger Fares: Passenger fares and airmail rates for the Shanghai-Hankou line remain unchanged. The fare from Hankou to Shashi is 58 yuan per person for a one-way ticket and 98 yuan per person for a round-trip ticket. The fare from Hankou to Yichang is 87 yuan per person for a one-way ticket and 148 yuan per person for a round-trip ticket. For letters sent from Shanghai to Shashi and Yichang, in addition to regular postage, each item weighing less than 20 grams requires an additional airmail fee of 30 cents.

Beijing-Pingjin Air Route: As for the Beijing-Pingjin air route of the China National Aviation Corporation, although the radio stations in Tianjin and Xuzhou have been completely installed, the radio station in Beijing has not yet been transported, and the radio station in Jinan has also not been transported. Therefore, the date for the official inaugural flight is still difficult to determine. It is heard that the company is actively preparing for the Beijing-Pingjin line, striving to implement the flight as soon as possible.

Discussion on the Closing Account Period for the Money Trade 108

Colleagues in various ports responded enthusiastically

The Money Trade Association, for the sake of the Municipal Social Bureau's proposal that the annual accounting period for national industry and commerce be fixed starting from the 20th year of the Republic (1931) with the first period ending at the end of June, the second at the end of October, and the third at the end of February of the following year, held a meeting to discuss it. The members all said that there were various obstacles to the third closing account period ending at the end of February, and considered the end of January to be the most appropriate. They also sent letters to various ports seeking their agreement (the original text and the progress of the letter were recorded in various newspapers). Now, various ports have sent letters in succession unanimously agreeing and expressing their willingness to support the effort to achieve the original goal in order to benefit commerce. The letters from the Money Trade Associations of various ports are recorded below. (1) Letter from the Nanjing Municipal Money Trade Association: In reply, on March 15, we received your association's letter and the draft letter to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce regarding determining the annual accounting period for national industry and commerce in accordance with the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau's proposal to use the end of February as the final closing account period. After your association meeting resolved that there were various obstacles to the final closing account period ending at the end of February and determined that the end of January was the most appropriate date, we were honored to receive your inquiry. After our association held a meeting to discuss it, the members all agreed that your association's proposal was very appropriate. After investigation, the end of January is the end of an agricultural solar term, which is still convenient for summarizing accounts, and there are no conflicts with various customs. Everyone unanimously agreed to comply and implement it. This special letter is to inform your association and we hope you will take note of it. This is addressed to the Shanghai Money Trade Association. (2) Letter from the Wuhu County Money Trade Association: Respectfully, we received your letter regarding the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau's proposal to change the annual accounting period for national industry and commerce starting from the 20th year of the Republic (1931) to have the first closing account and submission period at the end of June, the second at the end of October, and the third final closing account period at the end of February of the following year, which was inquired by the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce to see if various industries agreed. Your association believes that it is difficult to implement the final closing account period at the end of February and proposes that the end of January be the final closing account period. This consideration is thorough, suitable for commercial conditions, and highly admirable. In addition to the telegram (original text attached below), the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce unanimously agreed. Please take note of it. (The rest is omitted.) Attached is a copy of the telegram: (Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Respected Sirs: After investigating the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau's proposal to use the end of February as the final closing account period, there are indeed various obstacles in commerce. Your association's inquiry of various industries' opinions is also insightful. Your city's Money Trade Association's proposal to use the end of January as the final closing account period is suitable for commercial conditions and our association highly agrees with it. Shanghai holds the commercial hub of the Yangtze River. This change in the closing account period was also proposed by your city's Social Bureau. Please accommodate the opinion of the money trade and vigorously advocate for it. The money trade is fortunate, and all industries are fortunate. The Wuhu County Money Trade Association respectfully expresses its gratitude.)

Shanghai County Farmers' Association Established Yesterday 109

Elected Executive Director and Executive Committee Members

The preparations for the Shanghai County Farmers' Association have been going on for a long time. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, the founding meeting was held in the auditorium of the County Reorganization Committee. Attendees included He Qingmei and Gu Yunru from the Second District, Jin Lemao and Huang Xueshang from the Third District, Wang Xiangmei and Ye Junde from the Fourth District, Zhu Daquan and Zhu Bochun from the Fifth District, Jiang Yanchou, instructor of the County Reorganization Committee, and Zhu Shifang, representative of the County Government. Zhu Daquan was publicly elected as the chairman, Huang Xueshang as the recorder. After the ceremony was conducted in accordance with regulations, the chairman first reported that the establishment of the Farmers' Association had been organized in four districts in the county. According to Article 13 of the County Farmers' Association's organizational regulations, it was possible to establish the County Farmers' Association. Thus, Comrade Gu Yunru and others initiated the preparations, which have now been organized and established. Next, the instructor of the County Reorganization Committee delivered an encouraging speech, saying that the establishment of the association today represented the spiritual hope of all farmers in Shanghai County. In the past, the farmers of Shanghai County, because they had no organization, had nowhere to express their grievances and nowhere to voice their opinions. However, these two problems would be solved in the future. However, he also hoped that everyone would pay attention to the following two points: (1) Farmers account for more than 90 percent of the county's population, but only a small number of them are members of the association. It is hoped that the association will work hard to recruit new members so that all farmers in the county are members of the association, and then the association's power will be more substantial. (2) In accordance with the Central Farmers' Association Law, various undertakings must be earnestly led, and farmers throughout the county must jointly study and work hard to implement them in order to develop the rural economy and consolidate the foundation of the country. Next, the county government representative delivered a speech (omitted). Then, elections were held, and as a result, Gu Yunru was elected as the Executive Director, Jin Lemao as the Deputy Executive Director, and Huang Xueshi, Zhu Daquan, Wang Xiangmei, Zhu Bochun, He Qingmei, and others as Executive Committee Members, and Ye Junde and Jin Linrong as Alternate Executive Committee Members. Gu Yunru, the representative attending the Provincial Farmers' Association, was elected. After the election, two temporary proposals were made: (1) How to receive various documents and accounts from the former County Farmers' Reorganization Committee. It was resolved that the Executive Committee would handle it. (2) To stipulate the association's regular expenses. It was resolved that the Executive Committee would prepare a budget and submit it to the competent authorities for allocation. After the meeting, the first meeting of the Executive Committee was held, and it did not end until around 6:00 PM.

Chairman Pan Rongting, representatives of the Preparatory Committee, and representatives of the former District Reorganization Committee delivered reports and guidance from superiors in succession. Then, elections were held, and Zhang Huishu, Zhang Huijun, Pan Rongting, Shen Junling, Zhu Hexiang, Zhang Yunlong, Cao Zuochen, and seven others were elected as Executive Committee Members, and Sun Liangxie, He Haosheng, Lu Mingzhao, Wang Zhang, Zhang Fuqing, and five others were elected as Councilors. The articles of association were discussed at the end, and then the meeting adjourned.

French Concession District: The preparations for the French Concession District Farmers' Association in this city have been completed. The founding meeting was held on the 29th at the Mingde Elementary School in Xujiahui, with 193 members attending. Liu Rong was publicly elected as the chairman. After the chairman's report, the articles of association were passed, and the officials were elected. As a result, Zhuang Yaoming was elected as the Executive Director, Pan Fengyuan as the Deputy Executive Director, and Shen Yunpu, Yao Xinqing, Gu Jinqing, Xu Xianshen, and Chen Yunlan as Executive Committee Members, and Liu Rong, Huang Simei, and Liu Donglin as Councilors. They were sworn in on the spot.

The Japanese Ship Xinqing Maru Suffers Repeated Misfortune 111

After Hitting a Reef, It Is Robbed Again

The sixth Xinqing Maru of the Japanese Osaka Shosen Kaisha, after its accident in the South China Sea, was robbed again. The details are as follows:

Japanese Ship Hits Reef: There are many hidden reefs in the South China Sea between Xiamen and Guangzhou. Last month, the Japanese ship Nasu Maru encountered fog and hit a reef there, and was subsequently robbed by pirates. This time, the sixth Xinqing Maru of the Osaka Shosen Kaisha, with a displacement of 3,400 tons, also encountered fog and accidentally hit a reef in the same area on the 24th of this month. The hull was broken and seawater entered the ship. Yesterday, it was learned that the entire ship was about to sink and there was no hope of towing it.

Hull Cracks: The No. 6 Xinqing Maru's first hold was first pierced by the reef, and the second hold was also caught on the reef. After water entered both holds, the hull sank, and the third hold also cracked, with seawater filling the cargo hold. Finally, the fourth hold could not support it either, and cracks appeared. All three holds were submerged in the sea, with only the stern still above the water. By yesterday afternoon, it was heard that the water had flooded the deck, almost submerging the entire ship.

Pirates Loot: After the accident, all the workers on the ship, totaling over a hundred, were rushing to the deck to try to launch the lifeboats to escape, when suddenly more than ten pirate-driven sailing ships, each carrying between twenty and thirty pirates, surrounded the Japanese ship in an attempt to loot it. At this time, the crew and sailors could not escape, so they obtained the prepared firearms from the captain's cabin and engaged in a fierce battle with the pirates, exchanging gunfire. Many sailors were wounded or killed.

Japanese Warship Rescues: After the accident, the captain first sent a radio message for help. After receiving the report, its Moji branch dispatched the rescue ship Yuusho, carrying 28 workers and technicians, to rescue the crew and inspect the towing situation. At the same time, the Japanese warship stationed in Magong also received the telegram and, after hearing that hundreds of pirates were besieging and attempting to loot the ship, two Magong warships rushed to the scene of the accident to protect the ship and rescue the distressed crew. Subsequently, it was heard that the Japanese warships had arrived at the South China Sea on the 29th. The pirates fled when the warships arrived. The crew was trying to rescue the ship, but the number of deaths and missing persons was still unknown. The entire ship's cargo and the ship itself had already completely sunk into the sea.

The Xinchang Ship Cannot Be Salvaged 112

At the memorial service of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company yesterday, engineer Zhang Yao reported that after inspecting the Xinchang at Sijiao Mountain, which had already sunk into the sea, the hull was cracked and could not be salvaged. The original plan had to be abandoned. The procedures for engaging a Japanese salvage company had also been terminated.

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jiang Yu Steamer Workers All Go on Strike 113

Unable to Sail This Morning

The Jiang Yu steamer of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, which departed from Shanghai for Hankou yesterday, saw its entire crew suddenly cease work in the afternoon, initiating a strike that resulted in the obstruction of cargo loading. The details of this matter have been investigated and reported as follows:

Transfer of Boatswain Triggers Strike

The Jiang Yu steamer, after returning to Shanghai from the Transportation Department, was scheduled to resume its Yangtze River route and depart this morning. The Navigation Department of the company issued an order yesterday promoting the boatswain of the steamer to a wharf position in another port, with a corresponding increase in salary. Unexpectedly, this decision sparked labor unrest and led to the strike.

Universal Opposition from Workers

Upon receiving this order, all the crew members on board the ship unanimously opposed it. The sailors, stokers, stewards, tallymen, and workers from the midship section collectively resolved to demand that the company rescind the order. They elected representatives to appeal to the responsible department, requesting the exemption of the boatswain from the transfer. However, the company, believing that yielding to the workers on the transfer of a single boatswain would set a difficult precedent, refused their request. Consequently, the entire crew declared a strike at 4:00 PM, ceasing all work.

Complete Disruption of Goods

Yesterday, a large quantity of goods was to be loaded onto the Jiang Yu steamer, and they were continuously transported to the Jinliyuan Wharf before 4:00 PM in preparation for loading. However, the sudden strike disrupted everything, leaving the wharf piled high with goods that could not be loaded onto the ship. Passengers who learned of the situation rushed to the company to inquire. The company, upon receiving the news, immediately dispatched personnel from the Navigation and Business Departments to persuade the workers to return to work.

Public Association Mediation Ineffective

After the incident, the workers reported it to the Shanghai branch of the Seamen's Union. Based on the report, the union immediately sent a letter to the head office, urging the company to quickly withdraw the order to transfer the boatswain, otherwise the strike might escalate. They requested an immediate response. The situation was tense, and as of 6:00 PM, there was still no resolution. By 8:00 PM that night, there was still no news of the Jiang Yu steamer departing, indicating that the issue had not yet been resolved.

Maritime Insurance Established for Seamen 114

Shanghai Chinese Merchant Shipping Companies have organized a maritime insurance company to provide financial assistance for the employees of merchant ships and to handle the aftermath of accidents. The initial organizers disbanded, but now eight shipping companies, including Sanbei, China Merchants, Ning Shao, etc., have jointly invested in the creation of a new one. They are actively drafting articles of association and raising capital. Last year, the seamen of various Chinese and foreign ships requested a pay raise starting in September. It was immediately agreed that each person would receive an increase of six yuan per month, with four yuan added from September and another two yuan in March of this year. Now that the second phase of the pay raise has arrived, the Shipping Guild has consulted with various shipping companies and obtained approval to add another two yuan per month to the workers' salaries. However, this additional salary will be reserved for maritime insurance premiums. The guild will invite representatives from the Seamen's Union to obtain the consent of the seamen to deduct these two yuan from each bureau's salary each month and send it to a designated agency of the Shipping Guild for safekeeping. Once the insurance company is established, insurance policies will be issued to each household. Yesterday, all the shipping companies were notified to deduct this amount from now on.
