During her days in Shanghai, every time she performed, the audience was packed, with no empty seats. Now, her tour in Bai Xia (Nanjing) is also extremely popular. People from all walks of life are eager to catch a glimpse of her beauty. Since Ms. Zi Luolan arrived in the capital, she has been warmly welcomed by all sectors, and famous people have been hosting banquets for her almost every day. The joint winter relief association of various sectors specially invited Ms. Zi Luolan to dance on the eighth. That day happened to be a day off, and the people of the capital, impressed by Ms. Zi Luolan's fame, created an unprecedented record of crowding and congestion to see her. Those who arrived late and could not get in were not few. On the evening of the ninth, Ms. Zi Luolan hosted a reception for newspaper reporters at the Shijie Hotel. A certain gentleman delivered a speech on her behalf, and his words were very appropriate. The guests all expressed their satisfaction. The next day, all the newspapers in the capital published extensive reports of thousands of words, praising her to the highest degree. Ms. Zi Luolan can be very proud of this. Starting on the fourteenth, she was hired by the Guomin Theater to perform for three days, two shows each day. The first day was "Mei Fei," "Wu Jia Po," and a toe dance. The second day was "Daiyu Buries Flowers," "San Niang Teaches Her Son," and an Egyptian dance. The third day was "Chen Miaochang Sits in the Palace" and a Zi Luolan dance. All of these are masterpieces of Ms. Zi Luolan's life. During these three days, the area around Yanggong Well was crowded with people and vehicles. The capital's entertainment venues have never been so lively, and it can be said that it broke records. As I write this, I recall a friend saying that before the Northern Expedition's oath-taking rally in the fifteenth year, Ms. Zi Luolan, although very young, was already famous for her songs and dances in the city of Guangzhou. Important Cantonese figures such as Li Jishen had already appreciated her and would call upon her to sing and dance to help boost the atmosphere at important banquets. When the Northern Expeditionary Army was about to depart, all the important figures held a banquet for Commander-in-Chief Jiang, who also summoned Ms. Zi Luolan to sing. Her melodious voice was like a new oriole coming out of the valley, and Commander-in-Chief Jiang applauded and praised her, saying to those present, "I hope that on the day of the Northern Expedition's success, I can listen to this song with you all again." Now that Ms. Zi Luolan has come to the capital, it is just after the pacification and unification of China. Commander-in-Chief Jiang may not have forgotten his previous words.

Travels in India (10) 161

— Ling Hua

On the 28th, Consul Lu and his wife invited me to dinner, and they also invited two friends from Ceylon (Sri Lanka). We had a lively discussion about the differences in customs. I was very interested and asked the Ceylonese people which is more likely to win in a fight between an elephant and a tiger. They replied that tigers are good at jumping. When fighting an elephant, they can jump onto the elephant's nose. Therefore, even though the elephant is brave, it is useless and it will be defeated and injure its head. From this point of view, it is not certain whether the previous practice of the Burmese people using tigers and elephants for fighting as a form of entertainment is a common occurrence. The Ceylonese people told me that elephants sometimes fight each other, but only male elephants fight; females do not fight. I asked how elephants are captured. They replied that they make a deep pit, place food on top, and cover it with dirt so that the elephant will approach the food and fall into the pit. After several days without food, they use five or seven people to pull it with iron ropes, and then it can be subdued.

The Ceylonese people told me that the customs of Ceylon are very different from those of India because there is no class division. In India, the four classes do not intermarry and cannot eat together. It is the strangest thing in the world. One day, I returned home late and had missed dinner. I thought of looking for a restaurant. I walked four or five miles and it was raining, but I could not find one. It was very strange. When I asked the Indians and Ceylonese friends, I learned that it was due to the caste system of Hinduism. People of different religions do not eat together, and people of different classes do not eat together. Restaurants cannot be opened for everyone, so everyone has to eat separately. The Ceylonese people told me that the strangest thing is that if a servant makes food for the family and the master has finished eating, even if there is a lot of leftover food, the servant will never eat it. They must throw it all away, start a new fire, cook again, and eat it themselves. This strange custom is incomprehensible. Also, tea from people of different religions cannot be shared, and even all objects cannot be used in common. There are many taboos. I find it very strange and think that the British should be very happy that they can permanently maintain this iron-clad system without change, which is for their submissive people. If these bad customs are not changed, I do not believe that the Indians can be free. An Indian told me that if the Indian caste system (i.e., caste) wants to be washed away, it will have to wait until Russian culture sweeps it away completely.

On the 29th, Saturday morning, I read about the World Religious Federation's anti-war conference in Geneva. Chen Huanzhang of Peking Confucius University also attended and gave a speech explaining the meaning of benevolence and love in the Spring and Autumn Annals. Xin Hanjun, the secretary of the Mahayana Buddhist Association, showed me a historical map of the life of Buddha, which was very interesting. I began to feel a deep sense of understanding. In the afternoon, the clerk, Bao Mike (J. Bhoumick), accompanied me to the zoo. We took a streetcar from the side of the university and changed cars once to get to (Kidderpore). After getting off, it cost two annas per person and we walked more than a hundred steps to get there. Buying a ticket cost one anna to enter. The clear stream in the big pond was very lovely. Mandarin ducks were swimming. I immediately saw two tigers seeming to be fighting. I was reminded of my poem that the cat is a small tiger and the tiger is a big cat. I have rarely seen cats fighting and even less often seen tigers fighting, except for people scolding tigers. In fact, the nature of tigers is much better than that of humans. When we arrived, they were indeed not fighting, but the two tigers were bathing and playing in the water, with only an iron railing separating them. From a distance, they appeared to be in the same pond. Further on, we saw two big elephants. The elephant is the largest animal on land. I once wrote a poem praising it. Its eyes are small. I bought bananas and held them in my hand on its nose, and each of them took the food to eat. The elephant is an herbivore like the cow. But I asked the Indian people whether there were any white elephants like the Buddha had, and they replied that they had not seen any. The birds were in the same large field. As soon as I entered, I heard beautiful sounds in the air. My Indian friend said that these were fairy birds, called Paradise Birds in English. They are beautiful and sing well. There are many kinds of parrots, some with colorful eyes and bodies. But the Beijing Zoo is not weaker than this. The price of buying a parrot here is not cheaper than in Beijing. There are many carnivorous birds. There is a kind of deer with four horns, each two feet long, two growing forward and two growing to the sides, which is also strange.

Gold Bar Trends Are Uncertain 162

Extremely Unstable Advances and Retreats Yesterday, March 30th, the gold bar market seemed to have slightly increased, but the market conditions remained uncertain. The difference between the high and low for the entire day amounted to eleven taels, mainly due to the stable trend of foreign exchange and unchanged prices. There were disputes between buyers and sellers in the market, but the buyers remained strong. Companies such as Da Xing Yong, Cui Chang Yong, Qian Chang, Xiang Cheng Feng Yong, and others were all buyers, while Fu Chang, Heng Xing, and Xin Heng mostly sold their positions. The slight rise in overseas silver markets did not have much impact, and the gold price showed a hidden upward trend. Later, due to the eager selling pressure and the apparent easing of exchange rates, the market was in a weak state, and the price plummeted by ten taels, dropping from 697 taels to 86 taels. Afterwards, the price fluctuated, sometimes rising and sometimes falling by three or four taels. However, the momentum seemed to be upward. The cash flow of various companies in the afternoon varied. It was initially stable, then firm. It was heard that India was selling a large batch of silver blocks, which caused the price to reach a peak. However, it fluctuated around four or five taels from time to time. Finally, the buying momentum was strong, and the evening market stood at around 696 taels. The spot price of bare bars remained stable, with the term delivery increasing by more than nine taels.

Liverpool's spot demand was very good last week. Futures trading was thin. Market conditions were unstable due to the US Department of Agriculture's lack of a clear statement. Currently, it is awaiting the development of new cotton. The Egyptian cotton market was calm and firm.

RICE MARKET IN GRAIN AND RIVER DEPOT IS SLUGGISH 171

Zhabei: Yesterday, around 30 boats arrived at the river depot. Due to poor sales, there were over 200 boats in stock. Therefore, although there has been cloudy and rainy weather recently, confidence remains bearish on white glutinous rice. The market trend was barely holding at the original level. Secondary grades were slightly reduced. The morning market also slightly tightened by a few points, but soon returned. Early indica rice was stagnant with no increase or decrease. Yangdu pointed rice and guest depot pointed rice were uniformly stable. Transactions were scarce, and the situation was sluggish. The change to cloudy weather made purchases of raw rice rare, and the appetite for purchases was very weak due to the cloudy weather. The overall market was stable with a hint of weakness.

South Shanghai: Yesterday, goods from various groups arrived in succession. Sales on this street remained stagnant. White glutinous rice from the northwest was sluggish because the sales yards in various places were quiet, and the atmosphere was weak. Fortunately, the cloudy weather prevented further price drops. Early indica rice in the south was in light demand, with ample arrivals and firm prices. Secondary grades were weak, only around 9.5 yuan. Yangdu indica was rarely transacted, and the market was quiet with no ups or downs. White raw rice was stagnant, but the market was stable because the inventory was not thick.

FLOUR MARKET IS EXTREMELY CHAOTIC 172

Covering Short Positions Recently, Leading to a Sudden Surge

For Distant Futures, Margin Calls Led to Large-Scale Selling

Yesterday, the flour market fluctuated up and down. Due to different goals and changing circumstances, some initially fell and then rose, while others rose and then fell. When prices opened in the morning, because foreign wheat quotations fell by 3-4 jiao, the mood was extremely chaotic. The lowest price for this month was 2 liang, and distant futures were all down 2 fen from the previous weekend. Later, this month began to recover, but distant futures remained sluggish. When the market opened in the afternoon, this month, because the short positions that had not been covered on the last day had to be covered, and because Fufeng Factory was taking back its positions, the price suddenly surged at the last moment, reaching a high of 2 liang and 4 fen. April also rose as a result. Most of the distant months were subject to margin calls. Customers who were unable to continue to deliver had to sell at a loss, resulting in a weak market. As a result, this month rose by 2.5 fen from the previous weekend, April by 5 li, May fell by 1.25 fen, June fell by 1.75 fen, July fell by 2.5 fen, and August fell by 1.5 fen.

THE REVIVAL OF THE WHEAT MARKET AWAITS 173

Yesterday, the wheat futures market was somewhat bleak because foreign wheat quotations fell by 3-4 jiao. However, many believed that the outcome in March was good, so if the arrival of foreign wheat eventually ceased, the pressure from short sellers might be slightly reduced. Therefore, there was still some calm amidst the boredom. Otherwise, the continuous decline in the flour market would also have a huge impact on the wheat market. However, rumors spread that a certain factory had ordered 3-4 more ships of foreign wheat at a price of only 3.8 taels, so the revival of the wheat market still awaits. As a result, this month fell by 4 fen, May and June fell by 2 fen, July fell by 1 fen, and August fell by 3 fen from the previous weekend.

GUEST RICE HAS A SLIGHT OUTLET TO SOUTHERN GROUPS 174

Yesterday, there was still no turnaround for guest indica rice. However, southern groups were slightly active, and the market showed some vitality amidst the stagnation. However, there was not much inventory, and high-quality goods were scarce. Guest groups had no choice, and there was no major change in prices. The overall market saw 200 bags of Jiangxi machine-milled early rice purchased by the Fuzhou group at a price of 11.8 yuan. There were no other transactions.

WOOLEN CLOTH AND TRIBUTE CLOTH CHANGED PRICES SEVERAL TIMES IN ONE DAY 175

The woolen cloth market continued to improve yesterday, with exceptionally smooth actual sales. Because cloth prices had turned from falling to rising, those who had been waiting and watching were now actively purchasing. In addition, this street took the opportunity to search for goods, and the number of those who pawned silver and transferred it to the station increased significantly in preparation for selling it in the autumn. As a result, tribute cloth and Zhongshan cloth rose sharply. Among the groups, the Qingdao group had the strongest demand. There were signs that the "Wild Goose" tribute cloth had been completely bought up. The price changed several times a day. In the morning, it was still selling for 3 qian and 5 fen, but in the afternoon, it reached around 3 qian and 6 fen. The "Four Gentlemen" from internal factories also rose sharply due to the increased unified tax and were selling for 2 qian and 9 fen and 2 li and a half. Zhongshan cloth also rose by 2 li and a half. Jiaoye title book cloth was 2 qian and 8 fen and a half, Huan Taizi was 2 qian and 8 fen, fine cloth rose again, Shuanglongzhu was 7 liang, 8 qian, and 7 fen and a half, Shilesidao was 9 liang and 1 qian, Yueyan was 9 liang and 7 qian, gray light twill jumped to 1 qian and a half, and Qianliju Jin Wengong reached 5 liang and 2 qian and a half. The outlet on this street was quite smooth. Hankou, the Yangtze River, Qingdao, and Tianjin were all actively purchasing.

Nichisha Sugar Opened 2,000 Bags

Yesterday, the sugar market's production area reported that the spot sugar price in Cuba had not changed. New York sugar futures fell by 2 fen in May and by a small 1 fen each in September and December. Java spot sugar also lacked volatility. The Public Association's Dutch sugar No. 24 raw sugar and white sugar saw slightly more active buying, and the market rose slightly again. Z Mark was 9 liang, 9 qian, and a half, YT Mark reached 8 liang, 8 qian, and a remainder, YR Mark was 10 liang, 0 qian, and 0.75 fen to 1 qian, Meiji was shouting 1 qian and a half, YRO Mark was 9 liang and 4 qian and a half, YS Mark was 10 liang, and TK Mark was 9 liang and 9 qian and a half. Although transactions were scarce, the market was firm. The Japanese sugar factory ship had just opened from Yanshuigang New Factory, immediately loading 2,000 bags of HZ Mark car sugar at a price of 3 yuan and 6 jiao in Japanese currency. New regulations such as taxes were quickly sold through due to the small amount.

GUIDELINES FOR ART SECTION SUBMISSIONS 178

(1) Text is limited to news, reviews, and introductions related to recent art (painting, music, engraving, architecture, drama, etc.) and literature, both domestic and foreign.

(2) Photos are limited to recent portraits of domestic and foreign artists and their works, as well as various photographs related to the text.

(3) The length of each text article should not exceed 2,000 characters.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(5) Manuscripts should be written horizontally. Do not write cursive script. Western texts should be abbreviated where possible. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(6) Do not use blue ink to draw illustrations in the manuscript, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black ink.

(7) Please indicate that the manuscript is for the Art Section Editorial Department.

(8) Submissions will not be returned whether they are published or not. If you require a return, you must state this in advance and include sufficient postage.

(9) Remuneration for text is divided into three types: 4 yuan, 3 yuan, and 2 yuan per 1,000 characters. Remuneration for books and photographs is the same per piece. Special manuscripts will be paid separately.

GUIDELINES FOR SOCIAL NEWS SUBMISSIONS 179

(1) Text is limited to news about science, industry, commerce, rural areas, hygiene, aviation, exploration, customs, or urban life, both domestic and foreign.

Books are limited to lyrical books about social life in various extremes.

(2) Photos are considered suitable if they depict seasonal events, landscapes, animals, people, and news-related photography. Seasonal landscape photography featuring women is especially welcome.

SHANGHAI MARKET

BUSINESS NEWS 180

▲The Dahua Farm at the end of Xiyao on Yokohama Road in Zhabei declares that the seedlings of flowers and fruit trees produced by the farm, which has been registered with the Ministry of Industry, are of excellent quality and guaranteed to survive. The prices are low. In order to promote planting, there will be a special sale at an 80% discount on all items before April 20th of the lunar calendar. A large number of exotic flowers recently shipped from the Ningbo headquarters are beautiful and exquisite, and all are available. Ladies and gentlemen from all walks of life are welcome to visit and purchase.

▲The optical department of the Sincere Company on Nanjing Road declares that it has received new and exquisite fast cameras in various styles, with delicate designs, convenient portability, accurate light, and precise construction. The prices are fair. Especially for other matters.

▲The Guochang Department Store on Nanjing Road declares that after the establishment of its own business department, the business has broken through previous records. It has recently added major expansions in local products from various provinces. The department store has recently organized a training class to rigorously train the trainees recruited last time so that both materials and talents can be perfected, and customers can get excellent national products and receive sincere hospitality. Zhu Changli has been hired as the director of the training class, and the class will be opened soon. The subjects of the training are tentatively set at five types: Chinese, English, Arithmetic, Commerce, and Business Methods.
